[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libxml2 HTML parser vulnerability was uncovered by a fuzzing harness: [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer reports a heap-buffer-overflow in the function `htmlSecureComment`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mHTMLparser.[0m[1;92mc:3591[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. During HTML comment parsing, a multi-byte write via `memcpy` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceeds the allocated buffer bounds. The overflow propagates through [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlTopParseComment`, `htmlParseDocument`, and `htmlCtxtParseDocument` before [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreaching the fuzz entry point in `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - A heap-buffer-overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmulti-byte write[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m detected by AddressSanitizer.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What happened  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The fuzzer invoked the HTML parser on crafted input.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - In `htmlSecureComment`, memory is allocated [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m501[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for comment content via[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlFuzzMalloc`.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - A subsequent `memcpy` call writes [0m[1;36m105[0m[39m bytes at an address just past the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated region, triggering the overflow.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability location and call chain  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. htmlSecureComment [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHTMLparser.[0m[1;92mc:3591[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. htmlTopParseComment [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHTMLparser.[0m[1;92mc:3700[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - ASAN trace pinpoints the overflow exactly at the end of the allocated buffer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;36m0x515000000775[0m[39m` is [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes past the [0m[1;36m501[0m[39m-byte allocation[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The fuzzer harness entry point simply calls the parser and is not the root [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The overflow occurs in comment-handling logic, suggesting a mismatch between [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer allocation size and the data length handled by `memcpy`.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Areas for investigation  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - In HTMLparser.c: the implementation of `htmlSecureComment`—how it computes and [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The `htmlTopParseComment` and `htmlParseDocument` routines to understand how [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomment data flows and whether any length checks are applied upstream.  [0m            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2838[0m[39m:            xmlChar *tmp = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mxmlRealloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer, newSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2839[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2840[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In htmlSecureComment [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHTMLparser.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the resize condition only tests `if [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, completely ignoring how many bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`used`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m have [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready been written to the buffer.  As a result, a small `buffer_size` can appear [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msufficient even though most of it is already consumed, allowing a subsequent [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`memcpy` of `extraSize` bytes to overrun the allocated region by up to `used` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By contrast, in htmlParseData the code correctly tests against the remaining [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspace [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`buffer_size - used`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and also enforces an overall maximum length [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`maxLength - used`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before resizing or erroring out.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy to Patch htmlSecureComment[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Incorporate “used” into the resize/overflow check:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace the existing[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        with the correct[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size - used[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        or equivalently[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + extraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        so that allocation is expanded whenever the upcoming copy would exceed the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer’s remaining capacity.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Enforce a maximum allowable comment length [0m[1;39m([0m[39mas htmlParseData does[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Determine or reuse the existing `maxLength` variable [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlikely passed into [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhtmlSecureComment or defined as a security option[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Before any copy or resize, insert:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > maxLength - used[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Report “comment too long” or “resource limit” error *[0m[35m/[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[1;35mhtmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[39m* or [0m[1;35mhtmlErr[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt, XML_ERR_RESOURCE_LIMIT, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               goto error;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        This prevents denial-of-service via unbounded comment growth and caps [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer allocation at a reasonable maximum.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Retain existing reallocation logic and error handling:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Keep the `newSize = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + extraSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m; [0m[1;35mxmlRealloc[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; buffer_size = [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnewSize;` approach, as it amortizes realloc calls and mirrors the pattern in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhtmlParseData.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Preserve any null‐termination and cleanup existing code paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe `error:`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlabel[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m so existing comment‐parsing logic outside overflow conditions remains [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munaltered.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open HTMLparser.c and locate the `htmlSecureComment` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3577[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Introduce a check against `maxLength - used` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimmediately after computing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`extraSize`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > maxLength - used[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mhtmlErr[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt, XML_ERR_RESOURCE_LIMIT,[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                    [0m[32m"comment too long\n"[0m[39m, NULL, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            goto error;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Change the resize condition:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        -   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        +   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size - used[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Leave the newSize computation unmodified, so it still uses `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Build & run existing regression tests to confirm no functional breakage.  In [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparticular:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Valid HTML comments of typical lengths should parse unchanged.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Overly large comments should now trigger a recoverable parse error rather [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthan cause a heap-buffer-overflow.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach directly mirrors the tested-correct logic in `htmlParseData` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m2830[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m2840[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, ensuring the buffer is only resized when the new data truly [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceeds the remaining capacity.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adding the `maxLength - used` guard prevents attacker-controlled inputs from [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mforcing unbounded growth or triggering repeated costly reallocations, aligning with[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibxml2’s resource-limit policy.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By operating solely within `htmlSecureComment`—no harness or test code is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodified—the change is localized, preserving all other parsing behavior and fuzzing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry points.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Extremely large but valid comments [0m[1;39m([0m[39mabove the configured `maxLength`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39myield a resource-limit error instead of being parsed. This is intentional for DoS [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefense.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - To mitigate user‐impact, document the default `maxLength` for comments and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallow it to be tuned via parser options if necessary.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to public APIs occur; callers still receive either a parsed buffer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor an error, as before.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - htmlParseData buffer‐resize pattern: HTMLparser.[0m[1;92mc:2830[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m2840[0m[39m.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing htmlSecureComment code: HTMLparser.[0m[1;92mc:3577[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3587[0m[39m.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzer entry remains untouched [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzz/html.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/home/qqor/crete/packages/python_oss_fuzz/.oss_fuzz/build/out/[0m[95mlibxml2[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m -v [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/tmp/[0m[95mtmp7l0qyyko[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m -t ghcr.io/aixcc-finals/base-runner:v1.[0m[1;36m3.0[0m[39m reproduce [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhtml -[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzer uncovered a heap-buffer-overflow in libxml2’s HTML comment parser [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mhtmlSecureComment[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when processing specially crafted input. An attempted patch [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroduced a bound check against a new “maxLength” limit and invoked `htmlErr` on [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow, but this change caused linker failures [0m[1;39m([0m[39m“undefined reference to [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlErr`”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during the build of command-line tools [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlcatalog, xmllint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA run of the HTML fuzzer against libxml2 produced an AddressSanitizer report [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshowing a multi-byte write beyond a heap buffer in HTMLparser.c’s [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlSecureComment` function. The overflow occurs when computing `extraSize = [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchunkSize + replSize` and copying into a buffer allocated based on `buffer_size` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly, without checking against cumulative usage. The sanitizer trace:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Write of [0m[1;36m105[0m[39m bytes at address just past a [0m[1;36m501[0m[39m-byte allocation  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Triggered in `__asan_memcpy` inside `htmlSecureComment`  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Allocated via `xmlFuzzMalloc`  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Called from `htmlTopParseComment` → `htmlParseDocument` → fuzz harness entry[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mKey observations:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The buffer is allocated to hold the immediate data but not the cumulative [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgrowth over successive replacements.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - No early check prevents `memcpy` from overrunning the allocated region.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The failure is reproducible by passing the same malformed input through the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhtml.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo prevent the overflow, the patch author replaced the original `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check with two conditional checks:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > maxLength - used[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Calls `[0m[1;35mhtmlErr[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt, XML_ERR_RESOURCE_LIMIT, [0m[32m"comment too long\n"[0m[39m, NULL, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Jumps to an `error` label  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size - used[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Computes new `newSize = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + extraSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m`  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Calls `xmlRealloc`[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe change aims to enforce an overall maximum comment length [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`maxLength`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempting to reallocate.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBuild Result After Patch  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRebuilding libxml2 with the patch failed at link time with undefined references:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • DWARF warnings: “invalid or unhandled FORM value: [0m[1;36m0x25[0m[39m”  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `[0m[35m/usr/bin/[0m[95mld[0m[39m: undefined reference to [0m[32m'htmlErr'[0m[39m` in HTMLparser.o  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Failures in targets `xmlcatalog` and `xmllint`  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The build aborted due to these link errors[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese errors indicate that the symbol `htmlErr` is either not declared or not [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlinked into the HTMLparser object, suggesting missing prototype or library linkage.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo fully assess and address the overflow and linking problems, the following [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodules and components should be reviewed:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. HTMLparser.c  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - The implementation of `htmlSecureComment`, `htmlTopParseComment`, and related[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer-management variables [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`buffer_size`, `used`, `maxLength`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - The existing error-reporting functions and their declarations [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., where [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlErr` is defined, how it is exposed[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - The `error` label and cleanup path to ensure safe deallocation and state [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistency.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Header and symbol exports  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - Ensure `htmlErr` is declared in an included header and exported in the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibxml2 build.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - Verify that all parser internal symbols are linked into the static library [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mused by xmlcatalog/xmllint.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Build system and configure scripts  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - Check whether new dependencies or defines [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., for `maxLength`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m require [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mupdates to Makefile.am or configure.ac.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - Confirm that the HTMLparser module is compiled with the correct object files [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand that symbols are not hidden.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHTML fuzz target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - While not the root cause, review how `xmlFuzzMalloc` and the fuzz entrypoint [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minteract with parser allocations to understand initial buffer sizing.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressing these areas will provide a comprehensive view of the buffer-overflow [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot cause and the linkage issues introduced by the patch.[0m                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3700[0m[39m:            buf = [0m[1;35mhtmlSecureComment[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt, MASK_DASH, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, maxLength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3701[0m[39m:            comment = buf;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview of the problem and root cause  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The heap-buffer-overflow in htmlSecureComment is due to missing a cumulative [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize check against the parser’s maxLength before copying new data into the buffer. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The previous patch attempted to add this check but used an undefined function [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlErr`, causing linker errors.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. High-level patch approach  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Revert the incorrect uses of `htmlErr` introduced by the last patch.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. In `htmlSecureComment`, immediately after computing `extraSize = chunkSize + [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreplSize`, insert a guard that compares the cumulative requested size [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`used + [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraSize`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m against the `maxLength` parameter.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. On overflow, report the error using the existing, linked function [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlParseErr`, not `htmlErr`. Then jump to the existing `error` label to clean up.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Retain the original buffer-growth logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlRealloc… [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m unchanged, so we only enforce the maximum length limit without [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maltering existing functionality.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed patch steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Open `HTMLparser.c` around the body of `htmlSecureComment` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3574[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3587[0m[39m in the original codebase[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Locate:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     chunkSize = in - chunk;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     extraSize = chunkSize + replSize;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Immediately after these two lines, insert:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Enforce overall comment length limit before any memcpy *[0m[35m/[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mmaxLength - used[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Report resource-limit error using the defined API *[0m[35m/[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mhtmlParseErr[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt, XML_ERR_RESOURCE_LIMIT,[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                      [0m[32m"comment too long\n"[0m[39m, NULL, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         goto error;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Leave the existing buffer reallocation check intact:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         size_t newSize = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + extraSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         xmlChar *tmp = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mxmlRealloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer, newSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         …[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove any previously added `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > maxLength - used[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mhtmlErr[0m[1;39m([0m[39m…[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblock.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Why this approach is optimal  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It mirrors the existing, tested pattern used in `htmlParseData` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msee lines [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2830[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m2834[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which correctly enforces `maxLength` using `htmlParseErr`.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It prevents cumulative overflow by stopping processing before any `memcpy` can[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverrun the buffer.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It uses only symbols already declared and linked [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`htmlParseErr`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, resolving [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe undefined reference to `htmlErr`.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It preserves the original reallocation strategy, ensuring that larger comments[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mup to `maxLength` are still accommodated.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness, test code, or external libraries are modified; fuzzing entrypoints[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain unchanged.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Preserving existing code logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The error path leads to the existing `error:` label, which restores [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ctxt->spaceTab` and `spaceMax` and returns NULL, matching the original cleanup [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - SAX callbacks and other downstream code are unaffected when comments are [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin limits.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only comments exceeding `maxLength` will trigger a resource-limit error, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexactly as intended.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential side effects and mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Side effect: Very long comments [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbeyond `maxLength`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m now consistently produce [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma controlled parsing error rather than undefined behavior.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: Users relying on extremely long comments may now get an [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXML_ERR_RESOURCE_LIMIT error. If needed, they can enable `HTML_PARSE_HUGE` to raise[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`maxLength` via `ctxt->options`.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No new dependencies or ABI changes are introduced.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References to code ranges for context  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Pattern in `htmlParseData` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcorrect use of htmlParseErr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     <code_range>HTMLparser.[0m[1;92mc:2829[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2834[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reallocation block in `htmlSecureComment`:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     <code_range>HTMLparser.[0m[1;92mc:3574[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3587[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Call site using `maxLength` in top-level comment parsing:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     <code_range>HTMLparser.[0m[1;92mc:3698[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3701[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
